// local, will bang on it\r\n\t\t\t\tvar len = obj.length;\r\n\t\t\t\tfor(var i = 0; i < len; i++)\r\n\t\t\t\t\txml += objectToXml(obj[i], 'item');\r\n\t\t\t\tbreak;\r\n\t\t\t\t\r\n\t\t\tcase 'object':\r\n\t\t\t\t_nodeName = _nodeName ? _nodeName : 'struct';\r\n\t\t\t\tnodeClass = 'struct';\r\n\t\t\t\tvar objectToXml = commonspot.util.xml.objectToXml;
